| Change Mute Switch Pixaroma (cascade rules, output type, originalModes ownership) | `js/mute_switch/` + `nodes/node_mute_switch.py`. State `node.properties.muteSwitchState = {version, selectMode:"single"|"multi", muteMode:"mute"|"bypass", rows:[{enabled,label}]}`. **Mute is JS-only** - no `app.graphToPrompt` hook. `applyAllMuteSwitches(graph)` (core.mjs) is the single funnel: walks every Mute Switch in the graph, computes each switch's `cascadeMuteSet` (upstream.mjs - direct-only mute + cascade through inner switches via visited-set), unions into `wantMuted`, writes `node.mode = 2 (mute)` or `4 (bypass)` on each member. **originalModes is graph-wide-distributed** - the FIRST switch to mute a node owns its `originalModes[id] = originalMode` entry; on delete, `restoreAllOnRemove` restores its own entries + re-runs `applyAllMuteSwitches(graph, excludeId)` so a surviving switch can re-mute and re-save. **Always save original even if `n.mode === targetMode`** (core.mjs:393-409) so users who manually pre-muted a node aren't stuck with no restore path. **Phantom `out` output of custom type `PIXAROMA_MUTE_CHAIN`** (Python `RETURN_TYPES = ("PIXAROMA_MUTE_CHAIN",)`, returns `(None,)` at runtime) - lets one Mute Switch wire into another's input (Mute Switch's `ANY` inputs accept anything including `PIXAROMA_MUTE_CHAIN`) but BLOCKS users from wiring `out` into non-Mute-Switch consumers (would crash receiving None). Schema migration in `normalizeSlots` re-adds the output if a workflow was saved before it existed (one-time dirty for legacy). All serialized writes are diff-gated (slot.pos, slot.label, slot.name, outputs[0].label, outputs[0].pos) per Vue Compat #18. Configure-replay gate `_pixMsConfiguring` + load-wide `isGraphLoading()` per Vue Compat #17 + #19. `_pixMsPatched` flag on `nodeType.prototype` prevents hot-reload exponential wrapping. Inline label editor uses the shared `installGraphUndoGuard` (Compat #6) so Ctrl+Z can't escape the input. `pruneOrphanedOriginalModes` runs at top of every `applyAllMuteSwitches` to drop entries whose upstream node was deleted. Empty `originalModes` is deleted at the end of `applyAllMuteSwitches` so saved JSON doesn't bloat. `_migrateState` shim + `STATE_VERSION = 1` exported for future schema bumps. |
| Change Switch Source Pixaroma (A/B banks, rows field, missing-side mode, editable labels) | `js/switch_source/` + `nodes/node_switch_source.py`. Two stacked banks: inputs ordered `a_1..a_N` (A block) then `b_1..b_N` (B block), outputs `output_1..output_N`, so `a_r` and `output_r` share band `r-1`. State `node.properties.switchSourceState = {version, active:"A"|"B", rows:N, missing:"connected"|"strict", labels:{rowIdx:name}}`. **Row count is set by the Rows field (NOT auto-grow)** - a labeled numeric box reusing the shared `makeNumericInput` (`js/shared/resize_panel.mjs`) wrapped with an orange "Rows" inline label; changing it calls `core.mjs::rebuildSlots(node, rows)` which removes ALL slots and re-adds them in two-bank order while PRESERVING links by snapshotting each wired slot's endpoint by name and reconnecting after (gated by `_pixSsRebuilding` so the connect/disconnect events don't re-enter the handler). Clamped so it can't drop below `highestWiredRow` (disconnect first to remove a row). Wire connect/disconnect NEVER changes the slot count - it only calls `updateOutputLabels` (type adoption + label, with the load-race guard so a wired output is never downgraded to `"*"`). Input slot labels are native "A"/"B"; output labels are the editable row name (else wire type, else `out r`) drawn natively from `out.label` - click an output label (hit-test `outputLabelRect` in `onMouseDown`) to open the inline rename overlay `js/switch_source/editor.mjs` (writes `state.labels[r]` + `out.label`; empty reverts to the type label). DOM control strip (`CONTROL_BAND` reserved height, `canvasOnly:true`): Rows field + A/B toggle (row 1) + Missing-side toggle "Use connected"/"Strict" (row 2). A/B toggle styling reused from Switch WH (`.pix-ss-btn`). `app.graphToPrompt` hook (bottom of index.js) injects `{version,active,rows,missing,aWired,bWired}` into the hidden `SwitchSourceState` AND prunes EACH ROW to the side actually used (active side if wired; in `connected` mode falls back to the other side; in `strict` keeps only the active side) so only that branch executes. Python `pick()` parses the state, returns the surviving value per row (`a_r` else `b_r` when active A, mirror for B), and raises a clear ValueError in `strict` mode when the active side is missing but the other side was wired. Configure-replay gate `_pixSsConfiguring` + load-wide `_ssLoadingGraph` (wraps `app.loadGraphData`) per Vue Compat #17/#19. MAX_ROWS = 16. Distinct from Switch (N-in-1-out, canvas-painted rows, per-row mutex) and Switch WH (fixed A/B W/H). |
| Change Prompt Stack Pixaroma rows / separator / sizing | `js/prompt_stack/` (index.js entry + core.mjs state + render.mjs DOM + interaction.mjs events). Python in `nodes/node_prompt_stack.py`. State on `node.properties.promptStackState` (rows array of `{id, enabled, label, text}`) + `app.graphToPrompt` hook injecting state + resolved separator into hidden `PromptStackState` (Pattern #9). Each row is a DOM widget block (`canvasOnly: true` per Vue Compat #15) with drag-handle, ON/OFF pill toggle (orange `#f66744` when ON, grey when OFF), editable label, textarea (auto-grows up to 120px then scrolls), and ✕ delete. `+ Add row` button below. | Change Prompt Multi Pixaroma rows / queue-loop behavior / mode toggle / size / outputs | `js/prompt_multi/` (index.js for queuePrompt patch + extension wiring + graphToPrompt hook + DEFAULT sizing; core.mjs for state schema + MODE_QUEUE / MODE_LIST constants + setMode; render.mjs for DOM including the mode pill bar + hint text; interaction.mjs for events). CSS prefix `.pix-pm-*` keeps it isolated from Prompt Stack's `.pix-ps-*`. Visual UX of rows mirrors Prompt Stack (drag handle, ON/OFF pill, label, textarea, ✕ delete with `pixConfirm`). Default fresh-node: 2 empty rows both ON in Queue mode, size `DEFAULT_W = 420` / `DEFAULT_H = 290` with `CHROME_ALLOWANCE = 70` in grow/fit calculations so the action button row stays inside the frame. PIXAROMA_PROMPT_LIST custom wire type is duplicated as a constant in both `nodes/node_prompt_multi.py` and `nodes/node_prompt_from_list.py` (deliberate to avoid a cross-file import chain — keep in sync). |
| Add / change Prompt From List Pixaroma | `nodes/node_prompt_from_list.py` (single Python file, ~80 lines, no JS at all — uses ComfyUI's native widget rendering deliberately to stay tiny). | Custom drop-in fonts (user adds their own) | Users drop `.ttf`/`.otf` into `ComfyUI/models/fonts/` (auto-created at server import via `_font_catalog.get_custom_fonts_dir()`; redirectable through `extra_model_paths.yaml` — registered as a `folder_paths` "fonts" type). The shared `nodes/_font_catalog.py` is the single source of truth: `builtin_catalog()` (the BUNDLE) + `scan_custom_dirs()` (reads each file's internal family/style via `ImageFont.getname()`, derives weight via `derive_weight()` keyword map + italic via `derive_italic()`, groups by family) merged by `full_catalog()`. Custom entries carry `source:"custom"` and a collision-safe `id`; builtins win id collisions. Custom catalog is fingerprint-cached (filename+mtime+size); `invalidate()` clears it; `GET /pixaroma/api/fonts/list?refresh=1` forces a rescan. Custom font files are served by the path-safe `GET /pixaroma/api/fonts/file/{name}` route (realpath-under-dir guard via `resolve_custom_file()`). Frontend: `js/framework/fonts.mjs::urlForVariant()` picks the URL by `source` (custom → the file route); `refreshFontCatalog()` clears the session cache. The picker (`js/framework/text_editor.mjs::openFontPopup`) has a filter box + Refresh button + a "Custom" category group, and loads each row's own typeface LAZILY via IntersectionObserver (do NOT reintroduce a preload-every-font loop — it was the perf hazard for big folders). Both Text Overlay and Composer text layers get this for free (shared picker + catalog). Test the scanner with `python scripts/font_catalog_check.py` (prints `CATALOG PASS`). `.ttc`/WOFF and full variable-axis exposure for custom fonts are intentionally out of scope; custom variable fonts render at their default instance. |

| Save Mp4 Pixaroma — change widgets / encoder flags / output naming | `nodes/node_save_mp4.py`. ffmpeg binary resolved via `_resolve_ffmpeg` (imageio-ffmpeg first, ffmpeg on PATH fallback, clear install hint on failure). Frames piped to ffmpeg's stdin as raw rgb24 (no temp PNGs). Audio (optional) is written to a temp WAV via `_write_wav_pcm16` (stdlib `wave` + numpy, NO torchaudio dep) and passed as a second `-i` input so muxing is one ffmpeg call. Bitmap renderer is the SHARED `js/framework/text_render.mjs::renderTextToCanvas`; panel is `js/framework/text_editor.mjs` in `composerMode`. Python composites it as a plain image - NO text code in `node_composition.py`. See "Composer Text Layer Patterns". |
| Paint AI Background Removal panel | `js/paint/core.mjs` `_buildBgRemovalPanel` + `_removeBgFromActiveLayer` (button gated on `ly.sourceKind === "image"`, set by the `onAddImage` handler and serialized as `source_kind` in the layer project JSON). Dropdown built by the shared `js/framework/bg_removal_dropdown.mjs` helper (1.3.34) so Paint and Composer render identical model pickers (BiRefNet variants on top, rembg below). Reuses the `/pixaroma/remove_bg` backend route via `PaintAPI.removeBg`. |
| Change AI Remove Background dropdown (Composer + Paint, 1.3.34+) | `js/framework/bg_removal_dropdown.mjs`. Exports `fetchBgRemovalInfo()` (GET /pixaroma/remove_bg_info) and `buildBgRemovalDropdown({ container, info, value, onChange })` (renders `<select>` with `<optgroup label="Pixaroma BiRefNet">` on top and `<optgroup label="rembg">` below; inline `<a href=...>Download {filename}</a>` under the select when the currently selected BiRefNet variant is not installed). Default-picks via `pickDefaultModel(info)`: first installed BiRefNet variant in priority order standard -> HR -> matting, else rembg `auto`. Variant catalog and inventory come from the backend (`BIREFNET_VARIANTS` in `nodes/_bg_removal_helpers.py`) so adding a new variant requires editing that file only. |
| Change Load Images from Folder Pixaroma (folder picker / gallery / native dialog / one-by-one list output / resize) | `js/load_images_folder/` (index.js = setup + state + `app.graphToPrompt` injection + `refit` + native-dialog Browse handler; ui.mjs = node body + multi-select gallery popup + in-app folder-browser popup + CSS + `attachClosePopup`; api.mjs = `listFolder`/`thumbURL`/`browseFolder`/`pickNativeFolder`; state.mjs = DEFAULT_STATE/readState/writeState/sortFiles) + `nodes/node_load_images_folder.py` (OUTPUT_IS_LIST loader + per-file path-traversal guard + IS_CHANGED) + `server_routes.py` routes `api_lif_list` / `api_lif_thumb` / `api_lif_browse` / `api_lif_pick_native` (helpers `_lif_list_files` / `_lif_make_thumb` / `_lif_native_folder_dialog` + the Windows/macOS/Linux dialog branches, all via `run_in_executor`). See "Load Images from Folder Pixaroma Patterns (do not regress)" - OUTPUT_IS_LIST = one-by-one (NOT a queue-driver), resize reuses the shared `buildModePanel` engine with stateKey `loadImagesFolderState`. |
| Preview Image Pixaroma — change button or strip / grid layout / geometry / colors | `js/preview/index.js` constants at the top (`BTN_H`, `BTN_GAP`, `MIN_W`, `MIN_H`, `DEFAULT_W`, `DEFAULT_H`, `IMG_STRIP_GAP`, `IMG_STRIP_V_PAD`, `IMG_STRIP_BORDER_W`, `BADGE_*`, `LAYOUT_TOGGLE_*`, `COLOR_ACTIVE_*` / `COLOR_DISABLED_*`). Button rects computed in `computeButtonRects`, painted in `paintBtn`. Strip (single horizontal row) rects via `layoutImgStrip`; Grid (2D wrap, **iterate-and-maximise area**, exact match for native PreviewImage's `calculateImageGrid` in `dialogService-*.js`) via `layoutImgGrid`. Algorithm: for each candidate `cols` in `1..N`, compute `rows = ceil(N/cols)`, `slotW = innerW/cols`, `slotH = innerH/rows`, CONTAIN scale `min(slotW/imgW, slotH/imgH, 1)`, cellW/H = imgW/H × scale, area = cellW × cellH × N; pick the cols that maximises area. Cell DIMENSIONS come from `frames[0]` scaled (the iterate-and-maximise pass), then EACH frame is CONTAIN-FIT within its OWN cell (per-frame `imgRect`, mirroring `layoutImgStrip`'s fit): a UNIFORM batch fills its cells exactly (no letterbox, since every frame's aspect equals frames[0]'s), a MIXED-size batch (now common via Load Images from Folder Pixaroma) LETTERBOXES the odd-shaped frames instead of STRETCHING them (fixed 2026-06; it stretched before). `slots` stay the full cells (click hit-test uses `slots`, so the whole cell is clickable); the selection border + the `N/M` badge anchor to `imgRect` (the fitted image, not the slot). The whole grid is centered inside `innerW × innerH`. When `frames[0]` hasn't loaded, falls back to `1×N` strip and reflows on the next draw once `naturalWidth/Height` are populated. Layout selection in `createStripWidget().draw` reads `getLayoutMode(node)` which checks `node.properties.pixaromaLayout` ('grid' / 'strip') with fallback to setting `Pixaroma.Preview.DefaultLayout`. Per-node toggle icon painted via `paintLayoutToggle` (top-right, hover-aware, glyph shows the OPPOSITE mode = what you'll switch to on click). Buttons + strip live as `addCustomWidget`s (so they reserve vertical space, draw immediately on node-add, and Vue-compat works). Don't switch back to `onDrawForeground` (Vue Compat #1) and don't return `ui.images` from the Python node (LiteGraph would render its native strip underneath the custom one — use the `pixaroma_preview_frames` custom UI key instead, Save Mp4 pattern). |
| Preview Image Pixaroma — change save flow / routes | Backend: `nodes/node_preview.py` (tensor → PNG, two modes: temp/ for preview, output/ for save with embedded metadata via shared `nodes/_save_helpers._build_pnginfo`) + `server_routes.py` helpers `_embed_workflow_metadata` (thin wrapper), `/pixaroma/api/preview/save`, `/pixaroma/api/preview/prepare`. Both routes validate `filename_prefix` via shared `nodes/_save_helpers._safe_prefix` (denylist: neutralizes only Windows-illegal chars, keeps Unicode/spaces like native SaveImage, rejects `..`; locked by `scripts/save_prefix_check.py`). Prepare route returns JSON `{image_b64, suggested_filename}` — `suggested_filename` peeks `folder_paths.get_save_image_path` to pre-fill the Save-to-Disk picker with the next free counter. Frontend: `js/preview/index.js` `saveToOutput` / `saveToDisk` read the SELECTED frame from `node._pixaromaFrames[node._pixaromaSelectedFrame]`. Both POST a dataURL + the workflow/prompt from `app.graphToPrompt()`. Metadata embedding lives in `nodes/_save_helpers._build_pnginfo` only (single source of truth). |
| Preview Image Pixaroma — add / change save_mode behavior or hidden inputs | `nodes/node_preview.py`. `INPUT_TYPES` declares `save_mode` as a required combo (`preview` / `save`, default `preview`) and `prompt: PROMPT, extra_pnginfo: EXTRA_PNGINFO` as hidden inputs. In `save` mode the node iterates the entire batch, calls `folder_paths.get_save_image_path`, and saves each frame to `output/{subfolder}/{name}_{counter+i:05}_.png` with embedded metadata — drop-in for native SaveImage. In `preview` mode it writes UUID-named PNGs to `temp/` (auto-cleared on ComfyUI restart). Either mode returns `ui.pixaroma_preview_frames` (custom key). |
| Notify Pixaroma — add or swap a sound | Drop a `.mp3` (or `.wav`/`.ogg`) into `assets/sounds/`, restart ComfyUI. `_list_sounds()` in `nodes/node_notify.py` auto-enumerates the folder at every `INPUT_TYPES()` call. No code changes needed. To remove a sound, delete its file. |
| Notify Pixaroma — change widgets / Python contract | `nodes/node_notify.py` (single file, ~80 lines). `INPUT_TYPES` declares `any` (AnyType wire), `enabled` (BOOLEAN), `sound` (combo from `_list_sounds()`), `volume` (INT 0-100), `label` (STRING). `IS_CHANGED` returns `float("nan")` so the node always re-executes (notification fires on every Run, even when upstream is fully cached). `notify()` returns `{"ui": {"pixaroma_notify": [{sound, volume, label}]}}` when enabled, else `{"ui": {}}`. AnyType class overrides `__ne__` to bypass ComfyUI's strict type matching. Per-node `enabled=false` is symmetric silent on Python and JS (no print, no event). |
| Notify Pixaroma — change JS audio / Preview button / Settings | `js/notify/index.js` (single file, ~65 lines). `playSound(filename, volume01)` helper builds URL `/pixaroma/assets/sounds/<name>` and `<audio>.play()`s. `app.registerExtension` declares the master toggle `Pixaroma.Notify.Enabled` under category `["👑 Pixaroma", "Notify"]`. `setup()` registers ONE global `api.addEventListener("executed", ...)` listener that reads `pixaroma_notify` and gates on the master setting. `beforeRegisterNodeDef` adds a native `▶ Preview` button via `addWidget("button", ...)` that bypasses both master and per-node toggles (manual override - the user is actively asking to hear the sound now; toggles only gate automatic notifications during workflow runs). |
| Prompt Reader Pixaroma — extraction logic (PNG chunks, workflow walk, A1111 parser) | `nodes/_prompt_reader_helpers.py`. `read_prompt_from_image(path)` is the single entry point — returns `{found, text, source}` or `{found, message}`. PNG chunks via `PIL.Image.open(...).info`. ComfyUI workflow walker: find sampler-class nodes (`/sampler/i`), follow `positive` input backwards via `_walk_for_text` (DFS with `_MAX_WALK_DEPTH = 24` cap + visited set). `_TEXT_KEYS` (frozenset, O(1) membership) lists every input name that can carry prompt text (text, text_g, text_l, text_a, text_b, string, prompt, value, etc.) — add to the set when ComfyUI introduces new prompt-bearing widget names. `_COND_LINK_KEYS` is the smaller set of inputs the walker follows for conditioning chains (ConditioningCombine etc.). A1111 fallback: split on `\nNegative prompt:` or the first known param line (`Steps:`, `Sampler:`, etc.). See Prompt Reader Pixaroma Patterns #9 and #10. |
| Prompt Reader Pixaroma — node widgets / Python contract / IS_CHANGED | `nodes/node_prompt_reader.py` (single file, ~75 lines). `INPUT_TYPES` declares `image` combo with `image_upload: True` (filled from input/ contents); no hidden inputs. `IS_CHANGED` returns `(st_mtime_ns, st_size)` — NOT a content hash; see Pattern #7. STRING output named `text`; when no prompt is found, the explanatory message also flows through the STRING output so downstream wiring doesn't see an empty string. `OUTPUT_NODE = True`. |
| Prompt Reader Pixaroma — frontend (upload, combo, readout, copy) | `js/prompt_reader/index.js` (single file, ~700 lines). Custom DOM widget with Upload button, drag-drop target, custom file-combo dropdown popup, monospace read-only textarea readout, status pill (with the orange Copy button), live-extract via `/pixaroma/api/prompt_reader/extract` on every file change. State persisted on `node.properties.promptReaderState` (Pattern #9 family). Default size 400×300 set in `setupNode` after `addDOMWidget`. The `node.imgs` override (defineProperty get/set) suppresses ComfyUI's native bottom-of-node preview — see Pattern #2. Race protection via `nextReqId(node)` — see Pattern #3. `nodeType.prototype.onRemoved` closes any open popup and bumps the reqId — see Pattern #4. `alert()` is NEVER used — all error paths flow through `applyResult(node, { found: false, message })` and surface in the status pill (Pattern #6). |
| Prompt Reader Pixaroma — live-readout / list-files route | `server_routes.py` `/pixaroma/api/prompt_reader/extract`. GET with `?filename=<name>` (optionally with `[input]`/`[output]`/`[temp]` annotation). Always returns 200 with JSON `{found, text, source}` or `{found, message}` so the frontend never has to branch on HTTP status. Path-traversal hardening via `_is_path_under(child, *allowed_roots)` — realpath both sides, commonpath check against the three folder_paths roots. See Pattern #1. |

### 3. When adding a new method to an editor class
- Add it to the most relevant existing `.mjs` file by concern (tools, events, render, etc.)
- Use the mixin pattern: `ClassName.prototype.newMethod = function() { ... };`
- Do NOT create new files unless the relevant file would exceed ~400 lines
- New module files must use `.mjs` extension (only `index.js` entry points use `.js`)

### 4. When creating a new editor
Follow the existing directory structure:
1. Create `js/<name>/` with `index.js` (entry point, `.js`), `core.mjs`, and concern-based splits (all `.mjs`)
2. Create `nodes/node_<name>.py` with mappings + `CATEGORY = "👑 Pixaroma"` (the prefix is what makes the node inherit the brand colors via `js/brand/index.js` — do NOT re-add per-node `node.color` / `node.bgcolor` guards)
3. Import and merge in `__init__.py`
4. If it needs backend routes: add to `server_routes.py`
5. Keep every file under ~300 lines

### 5. Do not read framework CSS
`js/framework/theme.mjs` is ~660 lines but ~580 are a CSS string literal. You almost never need to read it. Only read it if you're adding a new CSS class or changing the color theme.

### 6. Picking a default `node.size` — paste-into-console sizer snippet
When the user wants you to bake a default size for a new node (or change an existing one), don't guess. Hand them this snippet, ask them to paste it into the browser console (F12) with at least one of the target nodes on the canvas, drag-resize to taste, and report the W × H back. Then set `node.size[0] = W; node.size[1] = H;` inside the node's `setupNode` (or equivalent `nodeCreated` path) AFTER `addDOMWidget` — LiteGraph's `configure` runs after `nodeCreated` and overwrites `node.size` from saved workflow JSON, so existing workflows keep their saved size while fresh-on-canvas drops get the new default. Replace `<COMFY_CLASS>` with the actual class name (e.g. `PixaromaPromptReader`).

```js
(() => {
  const node = (app.graph?._nodes || app.graph?.nodes || [])
    .find(n => n.comfyClass === "<COMFY_CLASS>");
  if (!node) { console.warn("Target node not on canvas"); return; }
  document.querySelector("#pix-sizer")?.remove();
  const box = document.createElement("div");
  box.id = "pix-sizer";
  box.style.cssText = "position:fixed;bottom:20px;right:20px;background:#1d1d1d;color:#fff;font:14px monospace;padding:10px 14px;border-radius:6px;border:2px solid #f66744;z-index:99999;pointer-events:none;";
  document.body.appendChild(box);
  const update = () => { box.textContent = `${node.comfyClass}: ${Math.round(node.size[0])} × ${Math.round(node.size[1])}`; };
  update();
  clearInterval(window._pixSizerInterval);
  window._pixSizerInterval = setInterval(update, 100);
  window.setNodeSize = (w, h) => { node.size[0] = w; node.size[1] = h; app.graph.setDirtyCanvas(true, true); update(); };
  window.removePixSizer = () => { clearInterval(window._pixSizerInterval); document.querySelector("#pix-sizer")?.remove(); };
  console.log("Drag-resize and watch the bottom-right corner. setNodeSize(w, h) to set exact. removePixSizer() to hide.");
})();
```

Defaults should reflect the node's CONTENT, not a generic minimum. A text-heavy readout node (Prompt Reader Pixaroma) wants ~400 × 300 so a typical prompt is visible without scrolling; a compact control node (Resolution Pixaroma, Switch WH) wants something smaller. Always ask the user — taste is per-node.

## Important Note
After major changes, please update this file (@CLUADE.me). Keep this file up-to-date with the project's status.

## Git Workflow

Home is now **GitLab** (`gitlab.com/pixaroma/comfyui-pixaroma`); the GitHub remote is suspended, so "push" means GitLab. The user develops on a working branch (historically `Ioan`, integrated to `main` for releases). Confirm the current branch with `git branch --show-current` rather than assuming.

1. **Local commits (default, no confirmation needed):** after any working change, make a small local checkpoint commit. The user relies on these to roll back (`git stash`, `git reset --hard HEAD~1`, `git checkout <sha>`).
2. **Push (only when the user explicitly asks)** ("push to gitlab", "push it", "release it"). Never push proactively.

**Pattern:** edit → verify it works → `git add -A && git commit -m "scope: description"` (local). Keep commits small and focused. Never amend a pushed commit; amend local-only WIP freely. If work breaks, roll back to the previous checkpoint.

**Release** is an explicit user trigger ("release it" / "publish new version"): bump the `pyproject.toml` version, merge the working branch to `main`, push to GitLab → CI publishes to the Comfy Registry. Add a README changelog entry (one entry per day, plain language).

## Publishing
The plugin auto-publishes to the ComfyUI Registry via **GitLab CI** (`.gitlab-ci.yml` + the `REGISTRY_ACCESS_TOKEN` CI variable) when a version bump lands on GitLab `main`. (The legacy `.github/workflows/publish.yml` is inactive; GitHub is suspended.) During normal work do NOT modify `pyproject.toml`, `LICENSE`, `.clauderules`, `.gitlab-ci.yml`, or `.github/workflows/publish.yml`. The ONE exception is an explicit release, where bumping the `pyproject.toml` version is exactly how a release is cut.
